# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}

## Example
```hcl

  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

# checkov Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}

## Example
```hcl

  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```

## Objective
Use Checkov to enforce security policies on Terraform configurations.

## Recommendations
- Run Checkov in your CI pipeline.
- Customize policies using YAML definitions.
- Fail builds on critical misconfigurations.

## Example
```hcl
checkov -d . --quiet

resource "aws_s3_bucket" "example" {
  bucket = "checkov-verified-bucket"
  acl    = "private"
}
```
